NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
L.K.S. Enterprises Limited
60, Usman Road, 3rd Floor, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017
NOTICE OF THE FINAL GENERAL MEETING
The Companies (Court) Rules, 1959
Form 155
Name of the Company: L.K.S. Enterprises Limited
Regd. Office No. 60, Usman Road, III Floor, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956 that a general meeting of the
members of the above named Company will be held at the registered office of the Company at No. 60, Usman Road,
III Floor, T. Nagar, Chennai-600 017 at 10.00 A.M. on 10th March, 2014 for the purpose of having an account laid before
them showing the manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the Company disposed off and
for hearing any explanation, that may be given by the liquidator and also for determining by a special resolution of the
Company, the manner in which the books of accounts and documents of the Company and of the liquidator shall be
disposed off.
Chennai,
31st January 2014

S. AKBAR SHAH
Liquidator.

R. Gopinathan, a male child born to D. Ramaswamy, residing at No: 218, Boobathy Nagar, Kamaraj Colony,
4th Street, Ambedkar Road, Kodambakkam, Chennai-24, has be living as female after a elaborate Sexual Reassignment
Surgery at Vela Hospital, Coimbatore as well as certificate issued by Dr. V. Jayaraman, Proff. of Plastic Surgery Head of
the Department of Plastic & Reconstructive Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College, Chennai, has made due medical verification
and issued a certificate. In this regard by this I may be treated as female and shall henceforth be known as R. SOWMIYA.

Chennai,
28th January 2014.

R. GOPINATHAN.
